## Websites Supported by JOJOFriend
JOJOFriend only supports the following platforms and matches URLs using the "Permission Pattern" matching method.

| Platform | Permission Pattern |
|----------|--------------------|
| 366 | ^https:\/\/([\w-]+\.)?366\.[\w.-]+([/?#].*)?$ |
